Yet, it remains unclear whether their performance reflects genuine legal reasoning ability or artifacts of data contamination. We present a comprehensive empirical study of tax law reasoning approaches and implement a contamination detection protocol to rigorously assess LLM reliability. We show that performance can be inflated by contamination. Building on this analysis, we conduct a systematic evaluation, comparing monolithic LLMs with hybrid systems that translate statutory text into formal representations and delegate inference to symbolic solvers. We build a novel test suite designed to probe generalization to unseen documents via case and rule variations. Our findings indicate that legal reasoning is inherently compositional and that neuro-symbolic frameworks offer a more reliable and robust foundation for legal AI, as well as improved generalization to unobserved situations.

</details>


### [133] [Sign-Separated Finite-Time Error Analysis of Q-Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16103)
*Donghwan Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对常数步长Q-learning提出了符号分离的有限时间误差分析。通过切换系统表示，将误差分解为负部分和正部分：负部分受与固定最优策略相关的低比较线性时不变（LTI）系统主导，正部分则由线性切换系统控制。分析表明，负侧LTI上界不慢于正侧切换上界，甚至可能产生更快的指数衰减包络。该研究揭示了Q-learning误差动态中的最大诱导不对称性，这种不对称性与过估计相关——正误差可被贝尔曼最大操作选择并传播，而负误差则受最优策略下界约束。文章给出了确定性和随机常数步长递推的有限时间误差界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Q-learning在实际应用中常面临收敛速度与误差控制的挑战，尤其是常数步长下的动态行为。现有分析多关注整体误差或对称性假设，但忽略了误差在正负方向上的非对称演化特性。本文旨在揭示这一内在不对称性，并提供更精细、更具区分性的误差边界，以深化对算法行为的理解。

Method: 基于切换系统理论，将Q-learning的误差分解为正负分量。负误差部分通过一个固定最优策略对应的线性时不变（LTI）系统进行下界刻画；正误差部分则通过一个线性切换系统建模。利用李雅普诺夫函数与矩阵不等式技术，分别推导出两部分的有限时间上界。结合两者得到整体误差的紧致边界。

Result: 提出了一种符号分离的有限时间误差分析框架，证明负误差的收敛速率不劣于正误差，且在某些情况下可能更快。揭示了由于贝尔曼最大操作导致的过估计偏差，即正误差具有累积和传播机制，而负误差受到最优策略的抑制。提供了适用于确定性和随机环境的常数步长Q-learning的严格有限时间误差界。

Conclusion: 本文通过符号分离的误差分析，揭示了常数步长Q-learning中固有的误差不对称性，强调了正误差因贝尔曼最大操作而被放大，而负误差则受制于最优策略的下界。该分析不仅提升了对算法收敛特性的理解，也为设计更稳健的强化学习算法提供了理论依据。

Abstract: This paper develops a sign-separated finite-time error analysis for constant step-size Q-learning. Starting from the switching-system representation, the error is decomposed into its componentwise negative and positive parts. The negative part is dominated by a lower comparison linear time-invariant (LTI) system associated with a fixed optimal policy, whereas the positive part is controlled by a linear switching system. The resulting bounds show that the negative-side LTI certificate is no slower than the positive-side switching certificate and may produce a faster exponential envelope. The analysis identifies a max-induced asymmetry in Q-learning error dynamics. This asymmetry is connected to overestimation: positive action-wise errors can be selected and propagated by the Bellman maximum, whereas negative errors admit an optimal-policy lower comparison. Finite-time bounds are provided for both deterministic and stochastic constant-step-size recursions.

</details>


### [134] [Property-Guided LLM Program Synthesis for Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16142)
*Augusto B. Corrêa,André G. Pereira,Jendrik Seipp*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出一种基于属性的大型语言模型（LLM）程序合成方法，通过检查候选程序是否满足形式化属性来替代传统的数值评分。当属性不满足时，系统会提供具体的反例，指导模型快速修复错误，从而大幅减少程序生成次数和评估成本。在PDDL规划领域实验中，该方法显著提升了合成启发式函数的质量与效率，平均减少7倍程序生成量，且在无需搜索的情况下解决更多任务，计算开销降低数个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于数值评分的程序合成方法缺乏对失败原因的解释，导致需要大量试错，增加推理和评估成本。为提升效率与质量，本文提出利用形式化属性进行引导，通过反例反馈实现高效修复。

Method: 采用属性验证机制，在生成候选程序后，通过测试集检查其是否满足预定义的形式化属性；若不满足，则返回首个违反属性的反例，供LLM用于修正程序。此过程构成一个迭代的反例引导修复循环。

Result: 在十个规划领域上，所生成的启发式函数几乎都能有效实现直接导向目标状态；相比最优已有方法，平均生成程序数减少7倍，无需搜索即可解决更多任务，候选程序评估所需计算量降低数个数量级。

Conclusion: 只要存在可验证的属性，基于属性的LLM程序合成能显著降低计算成本并提高程序质量，具有广泛适用性。

Abstract: LLMs have shown impressive success in program synthesis, discovering programs that surpass prior solutions. However, these approaches rely on simple numeric scores to signal program quality, such as the value of the solution or the number of passed tests. Because a score offers no guidance on why a program failed, the system must generate and evaluate many candidates hoping some succeed, increasing LLM inference and evaluation costs. We study a different approach: property-guided LLM program synthesis. Instead of scoring programs after evaluation, we check whether a candidate satisfies a formally defined property. When the property is violated, we stop the evaluation early and provide the LLM with a concrete counterexample showing exactly how the program failed. This feedback drastically reduces both the number of program generations and the evaluation cost, and can guide the LLM to generate stronger programs. We evaluate this approach on PDDL planning domains, asking the LLM to synthesize direct heuristic functions: every state reachable by strictly improving transitions has a strictly improving successor. A heuristic with this property leads hill-climbing algorithm directly to a goal state. A counterexample-guided repair loop generates one candidate program, checks the property over a training set, and returns the first case that violates the property. We evaluate our approach on ten planning domains with an out-of-distribution test set. The synthesized heuristics are effectively direct on virtually all test tasks, and compared to the best prior generation method our approach generates seven times fewer programs per domain on average, solves more tasks without using search, and requires several orders of magnitude less computation to evaluate candidates. Whenever a problem admits a verifiable property, property-guided LLM synthesis can reduce cost and improve program quality.

</details>


### [135] [An Algebraic Exposition of the Theory of Dyadic Morality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16153)
*Kush R. Varshney*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种代数化的方法来阐述二元道德理论（TDM），该理论基于一个简单的两节点模型：有意图的行动者对脆弱患者造成伤害。通过结构因果建模（SCM）符号形式化TDM，识别出三种心理操作符（类型化操作符、补全操作符和依赖于价值的推理机制），这些操作符扩展了标准SCM以捕捉人们在约束条件下计算道德判断的方式。针对TDM的二元局限性带来的可扩展性挑战，文章展示了道德认知如何通过节点坍缩和顺序处理压缩多节点场景。基于这一代数框架，文章展示了在人工智能政策设计中的具体应用：检测冲突义务、构建保持用户自主性的帮助政策，以及将故障后沟通设计为因果干预。最后，建议采用范围限定、情境化的心理感知测量，而非普遍平均，以实证操作化该理论。这种代数形式化使神经符号人工智能系统能够以数学严谨且忠实于人类道德认知的方式计算道德。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了更精确地描述和建模人类在复杂情境下的道德判断过程，尤其是面对涉及意图、伤害与脆弱性的二元关系时，需要一种既能反映心理机制又能支持技术实现的形式化框架。传统心理学模型缺乏足够的数学严谨性和可扩展性，难以应用于人工智能系统中。因此，本文旨在通过代数方法建立一个既符合人类道德直觉又适用于AI系统的形式化理论。

Method: 采用结构因果建模（SCM）符号体系对二元道德理论（TDM）进行形式化；引入三种心理操作符——类型化操作符、补全操作符和依赖于价值的推理机制，以扩展标准SCM；利用节点坍缩与顺序处理解决多节点场景的可扩展性问题；结合实际案例探讨其在AI政策设计中的应用，并提出基于情境的测量方法以实证验证理论。

Result: 成功构建了一个代数化的道德判断框架，能够有效捕捉人类道德认知的核心机制；证明了该框架在应对复杂道德情境时的可扩展性；在人工智能政策设计中实现了多个具体应用，包括冲突义务检测、用户自主性保护策略、故障后沟通作为因果干预的设计；提出更具情境敏感性的测量方案，提升了理论的可操作性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的代数化形式化框架不仅增强了对人类道德判断的理解，还为神经符号人工智能系统提供了可计算、可解释且忠于人类认知的道德推理工具。该方法兼顾理论深度与实践可行性，为未来人机共治环境下的伦理智能系统开发奠定了坚实基础。

Abstract: This paper provides an algebraic exposition of the theory of dyadic morality (TDM), a psychological model of moral judgment grounded in a simple two-node template: an intentional agent causing harm to a vulnerable patient. We formalize TDM using structural causal modeling (SCM) notation and identify three psychological operators (typecasting operator, completion operator, and valence-dependent inference mechanism) that extend standard SCM to capture how people compute moral judgments under constraints. We address scalability challenges arising from TDM's dyadic limitation, showing how moral cognition compresses multi-node scenarios through node collapse and sequential processing. Drawing on this algebraic framework, we demonstrate concrete applications to AI policy design: detecting conflicting obligations, structuring helpfulness policies to preserve user agency, and designing post-failure communication as causal interventions. Finally, we recommend scoped, contextual measurement of mind perception over universal averaging to operationalize the theory empirically. This algebraic formalization enables neurosymbolic AI systems to compute morality in a way that is both mathematically rigorous and faithful to human moral cognition.

### [136] [Formal Methods Meet LLMs: Auditing, Monitoring, and Intervention for Compliance of Advanced AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16198)
*Parand A. Alamdari,Toryn Q. Klassen,Sheila A. McIlraith*

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对黑箱大模型的行为监管缺乏有效手段，尤其在长期、复杂的时间依赖约束下，传统方法难以准确识别违规行为，亟需一种可信赖、可解释且具备实时响应能力的审计与监控框架。

Method: 融合形式化方法（特别是线性时序逻辑LTL）与现代机器学习技术，设计支持离线审计与在线运行时监控的框架；采用基于采样的预测监控方法，并引入可在运行时干预的监控器以预防潜在违规。

Result: 所提方法在检测时间扩展行为约束违规方面显著优于基准LLM方法；小模型标注器性能达到甚至超过先进LLM判别器水平；预测与干预监控有效降低违规率，同时保持任务性能稳定；实验揭示了LLM在长距离事件、多约束场景下的时序推理能力明显下降。

Conclusion: 本研究构建了一套高效、可扩展且可解释的AI系统行为审计与监控体系，适用于复杂动态环境中的高风险应用，为实现可信、可控的AI部署提供了关键技术支撑。

Abstract: We examine one particular dimension of AI governance: how to monitor and audit AI-enabled products and services throughout the AI development lifecycle, from pre-deployment testing to post-deployment auditing. Combining principles from formal methods with SoTA machine learning, we propose techniques that enable AI-enabled product and service developers, as well as third party AI developers and evaluators, to perform offline auditing and online (runtime) monitoring of product-specific (temporally extended) behavioral constraints such as safety constraints, norms, rules and regulations with respect to black-box advanced AI systems, notably LLMs. We further provide practical techniques for predictive monitoring, such as sampling-based methods, and we introduce intervening monitors that act at runtime to preempt and potentially mitigate predicted violations. Experimental results show that by exploiting the formal syntax and semantics of Linear Temporal Logic (LTL), our proposed auditing and monitoring techniques are superior to LLM baseline methods in detecting violations of temporally extended behavioral constraints; with our approach, even small-model labelers match or exceed frontier LLM judges. Our predictive and intervening monitors significantly reduce the violation rates of LLM-based agents while largely preserving task performance. We further show through controlled experiments that LLMs' temporal reasoning shows a pronounced degradation in accuracy with increasing event distance, number of constraints, and number of propositions.

### [137] [Fully Open Meditron: An Auditable Pipeline for Clinical LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16215)
*Xavier Theimer-Lienhard,Mushtaha El-Amin,Fay Elhassan,Sahaj Vaidya,Victor Cartier-Negadi,David Sasu,Lars Klein,Mary-Anne Hartley*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了首个完全开放的医学大模型决策支持系统（CDSS）构建管道——Fully Open Meditron，涵盖临床医生审核的数据集、可复现的训练框架和对齐实际应用的评估协议。该管道整合了8个公开医疗问答数据集，并通过三类临床医生验证的合成数据扩展覆盖范围：考试式问答、基于46,469份临床指南的问答及临床病例。整个流程实施系统级去污染、教师生成结果的黄金标签重采样和四名医师团队的端到端验证。评估采用基于大模型评判的协议，与204名人类评审者校准，结果显示所有基于该管道的模型均优于基础模型，其中Apertus-70B-MeditronFO在综合医学基准上较其基线提升6.6分（47.2%→53.8%），达到当前完全开放模型的新SOTA；Gemma-3-27B-MeditronFO在58.6%的对比中胜过MedGemma，且在HealthBench上表现更优（58% vs 55.9%）。证明了完全开放管道可在不牺牲可审计性和可复现性的前提下实现顶尖领域性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于大语言模型的临床决策支持系统（CDSS）普遍缺乏透明度，多数所谓'开源'模型仅开放权重，未公开数据来源、清洗流程和生成管道，导致难以审计和复现。医学领域尚无真正意义上的完全开放（FO）模型。为解决这一问题，亟需建立一个端到端可审计、可复现且对齐临床实际需求的完整训练与评估体系。

Method: 提出并实现完全开放的Meditron管道，包括：1）由临床医生审核的统一医疗问答数据集，融合8个公开数据集并新增三类合成数据（考试式问答、指南驱动问答、临床病例）；2）可复现的数据构建与训练框架，包含系统级去污染、教师生成结果的黄金标签重采样；3）四名医生参与的端到端验证流程；4）基于大模型作为裁判的评估协议，与204名人类评审者校准，用于评估模型在真实临床场景中的表现。

Result: 所有基于MeditronFO管道的模型均优于其基础模型。Apertus-70B-MeditronFO在综合医学基准上比其基线提升6.6个百分点（从47.2%到53.8%），成为当前完全开放模型的最新最先进水平（SoTA）。Gemma-3-27B-MeditronFO在58.6%的对比中胜过MedGemma，且在HealthBench上表现更优（58% vs 55.9%），证实该管道能有效提升性能同时保持完全开放性。

Conclusion: 本研究首次实现了医学领域完全开放的CDSS构建管道，证明了在保障可审计性与可复现性的前提下，仍可实现顶尖的领域性能。该范式为未来可信、透明、可验证的AI医疗系统发展提供了可靠路径。

Abstract: Clinical decision support systems (CDSS) require scrutable, auditable pipelines that enable rigorous, reproducible validation. Yet current LLM-based CDSS remain largely opaque. Most "open" models are open-weight only, releasing parameters while withholding the data provenance, curation procedures, and generation pipelines that determine model behavior. Fully Open (FO) models, which expose the complete training stack end-to-end, do not currently exist in medicine. We introduce Fully Open Meditron, the first fully open pipeline for building LLM-CDSS, comprising a clinician-audited training corpus, a reproducible data construction and training framework, and a use-aligned evaluation protocol. The corpus unifies eight public medical QA datasets into a normalized conversational format and expands coverage with three clinician-vetted synthetic extensions: exam-style QA, guideline-grounded QA derived from 46,469 clinical practice guidelines, and clinical vignettes. The pipeline enforces system-wide decontamination, gold-label resampling of teacher generations, and end-to-end validation by a four-physician panel. We evaluate using an LLM-as-a-judge protocol over expert-written clinical vignettes, calibrated against 204 human raters. We apply the recipe to five FO base models (Apertus-70B/8B-Instruct, OLMo-2-32B-SFT, EuroLLM-22B/9B-Instruct). All MeditronFO variants are preferred over their bases. Apertus-70B-MeditronFO improves +6.6 points over its base (47.2% to 53.8%) on aggregate medical benchmarks, establishing a new FO SoTA. Gemma-3-27B-MeditronFO is preferred over MedGemma in 58.6% of LLM-as-a-judge comparisons and outperforms it on HealthBench (58% vs 55.9%). These results show that fully open pipelines can achieve state-of-the-art domain-specific performance without sacrificing auditability or reproducibility.

### [138] [Prospective multi-pathogen disease forecasting using autonomous LLM-guided tree search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16238)
*Sarah Martinson,Michael P. Brenner,Martyna Plomecka,Brian P. Williams,Nicholas G. Reich,Zahra Shamsi*

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于大语言模型（LLM）引导的树搜索系统，实现传染病预测模型的自主生成、评估与优化。在2025-2026年美国呼吸道疾病季节的实时前瞻性评估中，该系统自主发现针对流感、新冠和呼吸道合胞病毒（RSV）的多样化模型，其集成模型表现优于或媲美由美国疾控中心（CDC）人工精心构建的基准模型。系统在数据稀缺的‘冷启动’场景下成功应对了RSV挑战，并通过消融实验验证了对数距离度量优化可防止奖励滥用，且引入自动化判官机制确保模型结构符合复杂科学理论。该框架将流行病学理论自动转化为准确、透明的代码，突破了传统建模的人力瓶颈，实现了专家级预测能力在前所未有的规模下的快速部署。

Method: 采用大语言模型（LLM）引导的树搜索策略，迭代生成、评估并优化可执行的预测软件。结合自动化判官机制保证模型结构符合科学理论，通过优化对数尺度距离指标防止奖励滥用，实现从理论到代码的自动化转化。

Abstract: Probabilistic forecasting of infectious diseases is crucial for public health but relies on labor-intensive manual model curation by expert modeling teams. This bespoke development bottlenecks scalability to granular geographic resolutions or emerging pathogens. Here, we present an autonomous system using Large Language Model (LLM)-guided tree search to iteratively generate, evaluate, and optimize executable forecasting software. In a fully prospective, real-time evaluation during the 2025-2026 US respiratory season, the system autonomously discovered methodologically diverse models for influenza, COVID-19, and respiratory syncytial virus (RSV). Aggregating these machine-generated models yielded an ensemble that consistently matched or outperformed the gold-standard, human-curated Centers for Disease Control and Prevention (CDC) hub ensembles out-of-sample. The system successfully navigated data-scarce "cold start" scenarios for RSV. Moreover, controlled retrospective ablations revealed that optimizing log-scale distance metrics prevents reward hacking, while an automated judge-in-the-loop ensures structural fidelity to complex scientific theories. By autonomously translating epidemiological theory into accurate, transparent code, this framework overcomes the modeling labor bottleneck, enabling rapid deployment of expert-level disease forecasting at unprecedented scales.

</details>

### [139] [Quantization Undoes Alignment: Bias Emergence in Compressed LLMs Across Models and Precision Levels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15208)
*Plawan Kumar Rath,Rahul Maliakkal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究通过控制实验分析了三种指令微调模型（Qwen2.5-7B、Mistral-7B、Phi-3.5-mini）在五种精度级别（BF16至3-bit）下的偏差表现，共涵盖12,148个BBQ基准测试项和5个随机种子，总计911,100次推理记录。结果发现，3-bit量化导致6-21%原本无偏的项目出现新的刻板行为，且呈明确剂量-反应模式；同时模型选择“未知”答案的意愿下降17.4%。然而，这些关键偏差变化在传统评估指标中几乎无法察觉：困惑度仅上升不足0.5%（8-bit以下）和低于3%（4-bit），但已有2.5-5.6%的项目在4-bit时已出现新偏差。这表明现有聚合度量指标严重低估公平性退化，强调需建立显式检测偏差涌现的质量感知压缩协议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型压缩依赖后训练量化以降低推理成本与内存占用，但其对模型质量的影响，尤其是对公平性的影响，尚不清晰。现有研究多仅比较全精度与单一量化版本，使用聚合偏差指标，并局限于单一模型家族，难以区分渐进式退化与阈值性安全失效。因此亟需更细致、系统性的评估来揭示量化带来的隐蔽风险。

Method: 开展受控的实证研究，选取三种指令微调模型（Qwen2.5-7B、Mistral-7B、Phi-3.5-mini），在五种精度水平（BF16至3-bit）下进行推理测试，覆盖12,148个BBQ偏差基准项，每项执行5次随机种子实验，共生成911,100条推理记录。采用逻辑回归分析偏差出现的剂量-反应关系，并对比不同精度下的困惑度与偏差变化。

Result: 3-bit量化使6-21%原本无偏的样本产生新的刻板行为，呈现显著剂量-反应趋势；模型拒绝回答‘未知’的比例下降17.4%。尽管困惑度增幅极小（8-bit以下<0.5%，4-bit以下<3%），但在4-bit时已有2.5-5.6%的样本出现新偏差。说明主流评估指标无法捕捉此类关键公平性退化。

Conclusion: 当前主流的聚合质量评估指标无法有效识别量化带来的公平性退化，尤其在低比特压缩下存在隐蔽偏差涌现的风险。必须发展具备质量感知能力的压缩协议，在部署前主动检测偏差生成，确保模型在压缩后仍保持公平性与安全性。

Abstract: Large Language Models are routinely compressed via post-training quantization to reduce inference costs and memory footprint for cloud and edge deployment, yet the impact of this compression on model quality remains poorly understood. Existing studies typically compare only two conditions (full-precision vs. a single quantized variant), rely on aggregate bias metrics, and evaluate a single model family, making it impossible to distinguish gradual degradation from threshold-dependent safety failures. We conduct a controlled empirical study of three instruction-tuned models (Qwen2.5-7B, Mistral-7B, Phi-3.5-mini) at five precision levels (BF16 through 3-bit) on 12,148 BBQ bias benchmark items across 5 random seeds, totaling 911,100 inference records. Our results reveal that 3-bit quantization causes 6-21% of previously unbiased items to develop new stereotypical behaviors, following a clear dose-response pattern confirmed via logistic regression, while models' willingness to select "unknown" answers declines by 17.4%. Crucially, these item-level changes are invisible to standard quality metrics: perplexity increases by less than 0.5% at 8-bit and under 3% at 4-bit across all three models, yet 2.5-5.6% of items already develop new biases at 4-bit. These findings demonstrate that aggregate evaluation metrics systematically miss fairness-critical degradation, underscoring the need for quality-aware compression protocols that explicitly test for bias emergence before deployment.

</details>


### [140] [MuteBench: Modality Unavailability Tolerance Evaluation for Incomplete Multimodal Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15235)
*Wugeng Zheng,Ziwen Kan,Tianlong Chen,Chen Chen,Song Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MuteBench 是一个涵盖 9 个数据集、6 种融合架构和两种缺失数据模式的基准，用于评估临床多模态模型在传感器故障下的鲁棒性。研究发现，模型架构家族是鲁棒性的最强预测因子，超过参数量；通道独立模型对模态缺失容忍度高，但对模态内缺失敏感，尤其在短序列上；课程模态丢弃仅在训练中使用过的最大丢弃率内有效；通道数、序列长度和模态对齐共同决定哪种缺失模式威胁更大；基于扩散的插补可提升分类性能，尤其对输入敏感的专家路由模型效果显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准无法在控制严重程度下评估多种融合架构在不同缺失模式（模态缺失与模态内缺失）下的表现，限制了临床多模态AI系统在实际传感器故障场景中的可靠性评估与设计优化。

Method: 构建 MuteBench 基准，覆盖 9 个临床数据集、6 种融合架构、2 种缺失模式，共 12.5 万样本，系统评估不同架构在可控缺失条件下的性能表现，并通过案例研究验证插补方法的有效性。

Result: 架构家族是鲁棒性的关键因素；通道独立模型对模态缺失鲁棒，但对模态内缺失敏感；课程丢弃仅在训练范围内有效；通道数、序列长度与对齐影响缺失模式威胁程度；扩散插补能提升下游任务性能，尤其对敏感模型效果显著。

Conclusion: MuteBench 为现有架构选择和未来鲁棒多模态融合方法的设计提供了实证指导，强调应优先考虑架构设计而非单纯增加参数量，并建议结合数据特性与缺失模式进行系统性优化。

Abstract: Multimodal physiological data powers clinical AI systems from intensive care units to wearable devices, but sensors routinely fail in practice. Two failure modes are common: modality missing, where an entire channel is absent, and within-modality missing, where a contiguous time segment is lost. No existing benchmark evaluates multiple fusion architectures under both failure modes at controlled severity levels across diverse clinical datasets. We present MuteBench, a benchmark covering 9 datasets from 7 clinical domains, 6 fusion architectures, and 2 missing-data modes over 125,000 samples. Through this benchmark, we find that architecture family is the strongest predictor of robustness, outweighing parameter count. Channel-independent models tolerate modality missing well but can be sensitive to within-modality missing, especially on short sequences. Curriculum modality dropout protects reliably only up to the maximum dropout rate used in training. We also find that channel count, sequence length, and modality alignment jointly determine which failure mode poses the greater threat. Finally, a PTB-XL case study suggests that diffusion-based imputation can improve downstream classification under within-modality missing, with the largest gains for models whose expert routing is most sensitive to corrupted inputs, though broader validation across datasets remains an open direction. MuteBench provides practitioners with concrete guidance for both selecting existing architectures and informing the design of future robust multimodal fusion methods.

</details>


### [141] [Reducing the Safety Tax in LLM Safety Alignment with On-Policy Self-Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15239)
*Yu Fu,Longxuan Yu,Haz Sameen Shahgir,Zhipeng Wei,Hui Liu,N. Benjamin Erichson,Yue Dong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: OPSA提出一种基于自监督的在线策略自蒸馏方法，通过模型自身生成轨迹并利用冻结教师模型进行密集的逐标记KL监督，有效缓解安全对推理能力的负面影响。引入教师翻转率以识别真正激活安全推理的上下文，提升安全对齐质量。在多个模型规模和架构上均表现更优，尤其在小模型上增益显著，且保持了更强的推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全对齐方法因分布不匹配导致安全与推理能力之间的权衡（即安全税），尤其是离策略训练造成的偏差。本文旨在通过在线策略自蒸馏解决这一问题，使模型在自我生成数据的同时获得更有效的安全指导。

Method: 提出OPSA（On-Policy Self-Distillation for Safety Alignment），让模型自主生成推理轨迹，并使用一个固定教师模型（基于特权安全上下文）提供逐标记的KL损失监督；引入教师翻转率作为信号，筛选能真正激发模型内在安全推理的上下文。

Result: 在两个推理模型家族和五个不同规模的模型上，OPSA相比离策略自蒸馏和外部教师蒸馏，在相同数据量和全参数微调条件下，实现了更优的安全-推理平衡；小模型提升最明显（如R1-Distill-1.5B +8.85，Qwen3-0.6B +5.49），且在不同训练集大小和对抗性越狱测试中表现稳定。

Conclusion: OPSA通过在线策略自蒸馏与教师翻转率机制，有效缓解了安全对齐中的安全税问题，不仅提升了安全性，还更好地保留了模型的通用推理能力，为高效、高质量的安全对齐提供了新路径。

Abstract: Safety alignment often improves robustness to harmful queries at the cost of reasoning ability, a tradeoff known as the safety tax. A common cause is distributional mismatch: supervised fine-tuning trains the target model on safety demonstrations produced by humans, external models, or fixed self-generated traces, rather than on trajectories sampled from its own policy. We identify off-policy training mismatch as a second source of this tax and study on-policy self-distillation for safety alignment, which we call OPSA. The model generates its own rollouts and receives dense per-token KL supervision from a frozen teacher copy of itself conditioned on a privileged safety context. Because this teacher must be safer than the sampled student trajectory, we introduce \emph{teacher flip rate}: a criterion that measures how often a privileged context converts unsafe responses into safe ones. We use this signal to search for contexts that activate latent safety reasoning rather than merely elicit safe-looking demonstrations. Across two reasoning-model families and five model scales, OPSA achieves a stronger safety--reasoning tradeoff than off-policy self-distillation and external-teacher distillation under matched data and full-parameter fine-tuning, with the largest gains on smaller models (+8.85 points on R1-Distill-1.5B and +5.49 points on Qwen3-0.6B). The gains persist across training-set sizes and adaptive jailbreak evaluations. Token-level analyses further show that OPSA concentrates updates near early compliance-decision tokens, providing a mechanism for improving safety while preserving general reasoning.

</details>


### [142] [Reading the Cell, Designing the Cure: Perturbation-Conditioned Molecular Diffusion for Function-Oriented Drug Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15243)
*Ziyu Xu,Zijian Zhang,Liang Wang,Zhiyuan Liu,Qiang Liu,Shu Wu,Liang Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于转录组的药物设计方法TBDD，将其视为生成式逆问题，旨在根据期望的转录组状态变化设计药物分子。针对生物学与化学之间的领域差异及转录组信号稀疏性等挑战，提出名为Cellular Response Engine（CURE）的多分辨率转录组引导扩散框架。该模型通过专门的转录组扰动功能特征提取器（TFE），从前后状态中提取功能导向的扰动嵌入，对齐双化学视图以弥合跨模态差距，并进行异质性感知聚合以从噪声数据中提取稳健的状态特异性信号。在标准基准和严格的分布外测试中，CURE显著优于现有基线，在结构质量和功能一致性方面表现优异。此外，通过零样本基因-抑制剂设计任务验证了其实际应用潜力，展示了表型驱动生成发现的前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当缺乏可靠的靶点结构或表型由调控通路失调引起时，转录组扰动可作为药物作用的系统级功能读出。因此，需要一种能够基于期望的转录组状态变化来设计药物分子的方法，以实现表型驱动的药物发现。然而，这一任务存在固有的不适定性，且受生物与化学领域间巨大差异及转录组信号稀疏性的制约，亟需新的建模方法。

Method: 提出CURE（Cellular Response Engine），一个基于扩散模型的多分辨率框架，结合专门设计的转录组扰动功能特征提取器（TFE）。TFE具备三项核心能力：(1) 从处理前后的转录组状态中提取功能导向的扰动嵌入；(2) 将这些嵌入与两种化学表示对齐，以缓解跨模态鸿沟；(3) 采用异质性感知聚合策略，从高噪声转录组数据中提取稳定、状态特异的信号。整个模型以生成方式解决药物设计的逆问题。

Result: 在多个标准基准和严格的分布外评估协议上，CURE均显著超越现有强基线模型，在药物分子的结构质量与功能一致性方面表现更优。同时，在零样本基因-抑制剂设计任务中表现出色，证明其在真实场景中的实用性与泛化能力。

Conclusion: 本研究成功将转录组驱动的药物设计形式化为生成式逆问题，并提出了有效的解决方案CURE。该方法有效应对了跨模态差距、信号稀疏性和噪声干扰等挑战，展现出在表型驱动药物发现中的强大潜力，为下一代精准药物设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: When reliable target structures are unavailable at scale or phenotypes arise from dysregulated pathways, transcriptomic perturbations provide a system-level functional readout for drug action. In this work, we formalize \emph{Transcriptome-based Drug Design (TBDD)} as a generative inverse problem: designing drug molecules conditioned on desired transcriptomic state transitions. We analyze the inherently ill-posed nature of this task, which is further complicated by the profound domain gap between biology and chemistry and by the sparsity of transcriptomic signals. To address these challenges, we propose \textbf{\themodel{}} (A \textbf{C}ell\textbf{U}lar \textbf{R}esponse \textbf{E}ngine), a multi-resolution transcriptome-guided diffusion framework. \themodel{} features a specialized \textbf{Transcriptome Perturbation Functional Feature Extractor (TFE)} that (1) distills function-oriented perturbation embeddings from pre/post states, (2) aligns these signatures to dual chemical views to bridge the cross-modal gap, and (3) performs heterogeneity-aware aggregation to extract robust state-specific signals from noisy transcriptomic data. Extensive evaluations on both standard benchmarks and rigorous out-of-distribution protocols demonstrate that \themodel{} consistently outperforms strong baselines in structural quality and functional consistency. Furthermore, we validate its practical utility via a zero-shot gene-inhibitor design task, highlighting the potential of phenotype-driven generative discovery.

</details>


### [143] [Privacy Evaluation of Generative Models for Trajectory Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15246)
*Stavros Bouras,Ioannis Kontopoulos,Chiara Pugliese,Francesco Lettich,Emanuele Carlini,Hanna Kavalionak,Chiara Renso,Konstantinos Tserpes*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究生成式轨迹模型与隐私评估的交集，揭示了现有生成模型在隐私保护评估方面的显著不足，并通过实施成员推理攻击证明其生成特性并不能消除隐私风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前生成式轨迹模型虽被认为具有隐私保护能力，但缺乏有效的隐私评估方法，存在隐私泄露风险，亟需系统性评估手段。

Method: 采用成员推理攻击（Membership Inference Attacks）对代表性生成模型进行实证分析，以评估其在轨迹数据生成中的隐私保护能力。

Result: 实验证明生成模型仍存在隐私泄露风险，生成性质并不自动保证隐私安全，现有评估体系存在明显缺失。

Conclusion: 生成式轨迹模型不能仅依赖其生成机制来确保隐私安全，必须引入严格的隐私评估方法，如成员推理攻击，以全面衡量其隐私保护性能。

Abstract: Trajectory data is fundamental to modern urban intelligence, yet its sensitivity raises significant privacy concerns. Generative models such as Generative Adversarial Networks, Variational Autoencoders, and Diffusion Models have been developed to generate realistic synthetic trajectory data by capturing underlying spatiotemporal distributions and mobility patterns. Although these models are often assumed to preserve privacy due to their generative nature, this assumption does not necessarily hold. In this work, we investigate the intersection of generative trajectory modeling and privacy evaluation. By identifying applicable empirical methods for assessing privacy preservation in trajectory generation tasks, we demonstrate a significant gap in the evaluation of privacy for generative trajectory models. Motivated by this gap, we implement Membership Inference Attacks against representative models, demonstrating the feasibility of using such empirical privacy evaluation methods and showing that their generative nature does not eliminate privacy risks.

### [144] [GQLA: Group-Query Latent Attention for Hardware-Adaptive Large Language Model Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15250)
*Fanxu Meng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出GQLA，一种对MLA的最小改进，使模型在不重新训练、无需自定义内核的情况下，通过运行时选择适配硬件的解码路径（MQA-absorb或GQA），同时支持H100和H20等不同硬件的高效推理，并实现多标记预测与零冗余张量并行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MLA虽高效但仅支持单一解码路径，限制了在非H100类硬件上的性能表现，且无法支持多标记预测与灵活的张量并行。为突破这一瓶颈，需设计一种可适配多种硬件、保持高效推理的同时支持更多并行策略的注意力机制。

Method: 提出Group-Query Latent Attention (GQLA)，在保持原参数不变的前提下，引入两个代数等价的解码路径：一是与MLA相同的MQA-absorb路径；二是支持每组扩展缓存的GQA路径。通过运行时动态选择最优路径，实现跨硬件优化。此外，提出TransGQLA方法，将预训练的GQA模型转换为GQLA模型，避免从头训练。

Result: 在LLaMA-3-8B上，GQLA在MQA-absorb路径下将每标记的KV缓存压缩至原始GQA基线的28.125%；在GQA路径上支持最多8路零冗余张量并行，并在H20上实现多标记预测增益。单套权重可适配H100与H20，分别达到各自硬件的理论峰值性能。

Conclusion: GQLA通过双路径设计实现了硬件无关的高效推理，在不牺牲训练效率的前提下，显著提升了模型在多样化硬件平台上的适应性与灵活性，是迈向通用化高性能大模型推理的关键一步。

Abstract: Multi-head Latent Attention (MLA), the attention used in DeepSeek-V2/V3, jointly compresses keys and values into a low-rank latent and matches the H100 roofline almost perfectly. Its trained weights, however, expose only one decoding path - an absorbed MQA form - which ties efficient inference to H100-class compute-bandwidth ratios, forfeits tensor parallelism along the head axis, and yields no Multi-Token Prediction (MTP) gain on commodity inference GPUs such as the export-restricted H20. We propose Group-Query Latent Attention (GQLA), a minimal modification of MLA whose trained weights expose two algebraically equivalent decoding paths over the same parameters: an MQA-absorb path identical to MLA's, and a GQA path with a per-group expanded cache. The runtime picks the path that matches the target hardware - no retraining, no custom kernels - so a single set of GQLA weights pins the rooflines of both H100 (MQA-absorb, s_q=1) and H20 (GQA + MTP, s_q=2), while supporting up to 8-way zero-redundancy tensor parallelism on the GQA path. To avoid pretraining from scratch we extend TransMLA into TransGQLA, which converts a pretrained GQA checkpoint into a GQLA model; on LLaMA-3-8B it compresses the per-token KV cache to 28.125% of the GQA baseline on the MQA-absorb path while structurally preserving GQA-level traffic on the per-group path.

</details>


### [145] [Position: Ideas Should be the Center of Machine Learning Research](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15253)
*Jairo Diaz-Rodriguez*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出“想法优先”（Ideas First）框架，主张机器学习研究应聚焦于核心科学对象——想法，而非单纯追求指标或理论形式化。通过设计针对性实验来验证想法预测的行为特征，而非争夺排行榜榜首。该框架有助于弥合理论与实践的鸿沟，并降低对计算资源的依赖，促进研究公平性。最终倡导以想法为中心的研究文化，将基准测试和定理视为检验机制假设的工具，而非终极目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器学习研究分裂为唯指标的工程化倾向与脱离现实的理论化倾向，两者均忽视了科学研究的核心：想法本身。这种分裂导致研究缺乏深度理解与可迁移性。

Method: 提出‘想法优先’框架，强调对想法的价值评估基于其在现代模型中预测的行为特征；设计定制化实验以检测这些特征，而非追求排行榜领先。

Result: 该方法能够连接理论与实践，减少对大规模资源的依赖，使不同背景的研究者都能做出严谨的科学贡献，推动更公平、更具洞察力的研究生态。

Conclusion: 应建立以想法为核心的科研文化，将基准测试和数学证明作为验证机制假设的手段，而非研究的最终目的，从而实现更可持续、包容和深入的机器学习发展。

Abstract: Machine learning research increasingly bifurcates into two disconnected modes: benchmark-driven engineering that prioritizes metrics over understanding, and idealized theory that often fails to transfer to modern systems. In this position paper, we argue that the field focuses too heavily on these endpoints, neglecting the central scientific object: the idea. We propose an Ideas First framework in which ideas are valued for the behavioral signatures they predict in modern models, and these signatures are tested through tailored experiments designed to detect the relevant patterns rather than to win leaderboards. This shift not only bridges the gap between theory and practice but also promotes equity by removing the "complexity premium," enabling rigorous scientific contributions from researchers with modest computational, financial, and human resources. Ultimately, we advocate for a research culture centered on ideas, treating benchmarks and theorems as instruments for testing mechanistic hypotheses rather than as ends in themselves.

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) monitoring is one of the most promising tools we have for detecting model misbehavior, but its effectiveness depends on models faithfully externalizing their reasoning. We also show that CoT controllability, a model's ability to reshape its own reasoning trace under an imposed constraint, is closely correlated with obfuscation success across the eight models studied ($r=0.800$, $p=0.017$). Monitor-aware models placed under equal reinforcement learning optimization pressure also learn to reward-hack without triggering a CoT monitor substantially faster than unaware controls. Together, these results suggest that knowledge of monitoring combined with high CoT controllability poses a risk to CoT-based monitoring.

### [147] [Tadpole: Autoencoders as Foundation Models for 3D PDEs with Online Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15284)

Abstract: We introduce Tadpole, a novel foundation model for three-dimensional partial differential equations (PDEs) that addresses key challenges in transferability, scalability to high dimensionality, and multi-functionality. Tadpole is pre-trained as an autoencoder on synthetic 3D PDE data generated by an efficient online data-generation framework. This enables large-scale, diverse training without storage or I/O overhead, demonstrated by scaling to an equivalent of hundreds of terabytes of training data. By autoencoding single-channel spatial crops, Tadpole learns rich and transferable representations across heterogeneous physical systems with varying numbers of state variables and spatial resolutions. Although pre-trained solely as an autoencoder, Tadpole can be efficiently applied for multiple downstream tasks beyond reconstruction, including dynamics learning and generative modeling. For dynamics learning, we propose a novel parameter-efficient fine-tuning strategy that integrates low-rank adaptation, latent-space transformations, and reintroduced skip connections, achieving accurate temporal modeling with a minimal number of trainable parameters. Tadpole demonstrates strong fine-tuning performance across various downstream tasks, highlighting its versatility and effectiveness as a foundation model for 3D PDE learning. Source code and pre-trained weights of Tadpole are available at https://github.com/tum-pbs/tadpole

### [148] [Universal Approximation of Nonlinear Operators and Their Derivatives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15285)

Method: 采用编码器-解码器架构参数化非线性算子，结合巴拿赫空间逼近性质、Bastiani k次连续可微性、紧开拓扑与新型加权Sobolev空间构造，证明了在紧凑集和加权范数下的通用逼近定理。

Abstract: Derivative-Informed Operator Learning (DIOL), i.e. learning a (nonlinear) operator and its derivatives, is an open research frontier at the foundations of the influential field of Operator Learning (OL). In particular, Universal Approximation Theorems (UATs) of nonlinear operators and their derivatives are foundational open questions and delicate problems in nonlinear functional analysis. In this manuscript, we prove the first UATs of non-linear $k$-times differentiable operators between Banach spaces and their derivatives, uniformly on compact sets and in weighted Sobolev norms for general finite input measures, via OL architectures. Our results are the first complete generalizations of the corresponding influential classical results in [Hornik, 1991] to infinite-dimensional settings and OL.
  We discuss several open areas where DIOL and our UATs find applications: high-order accuracy in OL, fast constrained optimization in Banach spaces (e.g. optimal control of PDEs, inverse problems) and numerical methods for infinite-dimensional PDEs (e.g. HJB PDEs on Banach spaces from optimal control of PDEs, SPDEs, path-dependent systems, partially observed systems, mean-field control).
  We parameterize nonlinear operators via Encoder-Decoder Architectures, renowned classes in OL due to their generality, including classical architectures, such as DeepONets, Deep-H-ONets, PCA-Nets. Our results are based on four key features that allow us to prove UATs in full generality: (i) Approximation Properties of Banach spaces. (ii) $k$-times continuous differentiability in the sense of Bastiani (weaker than $k$-times continuous Fréchet differentiability). (iii) Natural compact-open topologies for UA; indeed, we show that UA in standard compact-open topologies induced by operator norms is violated even for Fréchet derivatives. (iv) Construction of novel weighted Sobolev spaces for the UA.

### [150] [GESD: Beyond Outcome-Oriented Fairness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15295)
*Gideon Popoola,John Sheppard*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的程序导向公平性度量方法——群体级解释稳定性差异（GESD），用于衡量不同子群体在模型解释的稳定性、鲁棒性和敏感性方面的差异。该方法与解释器和模型无关，扩展了公平性分析的范围至可解释性层面。研究进一步将GESD融入多目标优化框架FEU（公平性-可解释性-实用性），以同时优化模型的性能、结果公平性和解释公平性。实验表明，GESD能有效捕捉解释质量的群体差异，且FEU在多项基准数据集上优于现有方法。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Machine learning (ML) algorithms are increasingly deployed in high-stakes decision-making domains such as loan approvals, hiring, and recidivism predictions. While existing fairness metrics (e.g., statistical parity, equal opportunity) effectively quantify outcome-oriented disparities, they offer limited insight into the procedure or explanation behind biased decisions. To address this gap, we propose Group-level Explanation Stability Disparity (GESD), a \textit{procedural-oriented} fairness metric that measures disparities in the stability, robustness, and sensitivity of model explanations across different subgroups in a protected category. %GESD is explainer-agnostic, model-agnostic, and extends the scope of fairness analyses to the level of explainability. We further integrate GESD into a multi-objective optimization framework that jointly optimizes for utility, outcome-based fairness, and explanation-based fairness called FEU (Fairness--Explainability--Utility). Empirical results on multiple benchmark datasets show that GESD effectively captures group-wise discrepancies in explanation quality, and that FEU improves both utility and fairness over state-of-the-art methods. By bridging outcome-based and explanation-based fairness, GESD offers a comprehensive tool for diagnosing and mitigating bias in predictive modeling. Our code and datasets are available on GitHub {\hyperlink{https://github.com/horlahsunbo/GESD}{https://github.com/horlahsunbo/GESD}}

### [151] [Beyond Bounded Variance: Variance-Reduced Normalized Methods for Nonconvex Optimization under Blum-Gladyshev Noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15314)
*Antesh Upadhyay,Arda Fazla,Abolfazl Hashemi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究在Blum-Gladyshev (BG-0)噪声模型下的非凸随机优化问题，该模型中随机梯度方差随与初始点距离的平方增长。考虑标准光滑性和对称广义光滑性框架，证明了仅需每轮一个随机梯度的归一化随机梯度下降带动量方法，在BG-0噪声下具有$O(\varepsilon^{-6})$的Oracle复杂度。该结果在标准光滑性和$\alpha$-对称广义光滑性下均成立，表明广义光滑性在此设置中对归一化动量方法无速率影响。进一步研究了一种归一化的方差减少STORM方法，在均方光滑性和尖锐初始化条件下，达到最优的$O(\varepsilon^{-4})$复杂度，匹配下界。在期望$\alpha$-对称广义光滑性下，由于梯度依赖光滑性与距离依赖噪声耦合，复杂度为$O(\varepsilon^{-(4+\alpha)})$（$\alpha\in(0,1)$）和$O(\varepsilon^{-5})$（$\alpha=1$）。当噪声模型中的距离增长参数消失时，结果退化为标准有界方差情形：动量方法$O(\varepsilon^{-4})$，方差减少方法$O(\varepsilon^{-3})$，确定性情况$O(\varepsilon^{-2})$。这些是首个在无界域、不增加批量大小或显式锚定条件下，针对归一化方法在非凸随机优化中BG-0噪声下的收敛保证，涵盖标准与广义光滑性场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非凸随机优化理论多假设噪声有界或使用固定大批次，难以刻画真实场景中梯度方差随迭代过程动态变化的现象。特别是当噪声方差随离初始点距离增加而增长时，传统方法性能下降。本文旨在建立在更现实的BG-0噪声模型下，无需强假设（如有界域、增大批次、显式锚定）的归一化优化方法的理论保障，尤其关注归一化动量与方差减少方法的收敛性。

Method: 提出并分析两种算法：(1) 归一化SGD带动量，仅使用单个随机梯度；(2) 归一化方差减少的STORM方法。通过引入新的技术工具，如对距离相关噪声建模、结合梯度依赖平滑性分析，以及设计适用于非标准光滑性框架的递推分析方法，建立收敛性边界。关键在于利用归一化机制缓解噪声增长带来的影响，并在广义光滑性下保持良好性能。

Result: 1. 归一化SGD带动量在标准光滑性和$\alpha$-对称广义光滑性下均实现$O(\varepsilon^{-6})$的复杂度，证明广义光滑性不影响收敛速率。2. 在均方光滑性和尖锐初始化下，归一化STORM方法达到最优$O(\varepsilon^{-4})$复杂度，匹配已知下界。3. 在期望$\alpha$-对称广义光滑性下，复杂度为$O(\varepsilon^{-(4+\alpha)})$（$\alpha\in(0,1)$）和$O(\varepsilon^{-5})$（$\alpha=1$），体现平滑性与噪声耦合效应。4. 当噪声距离增长参数趋于零时，恢复经典结果：$O(\varepsilon^{-4})$（动量）、$O(\varepsilon^{-3})$（方差减少）、$O(\varepsilon^{-2})$（确定性）。

Conclusion: 本文首次在无界域、无批量增长、无显式锚定的前提下，建立了归一化优化方法在非凸随机优化中面对BG-0噪声的严格收敛保证。结果表明，归一化机制能有效应对距离相关的噪声增长，且广义光滑性不会带来额外速率损失。此外，所提出的归一化方差减少方法在理想条件下可达到最优复杂度，为实际应用提供了强有力的理论支持。

Abstract: We study nonconvex stochastic optimization under the Blum-Gladyshev ($\mathsf{BG}$-0) noise model, where the stochastic gradient variance grows quadratically with the distance from the initialization. We consider this problem under both standard smoothness and the symmetric generalized-smoothness framework, which captures objectives whose local curvature can scale with the gradient norm. We prove that normalized stochastic gradient descent with momentum, using only one stochastic gradient per iteration, converges under $\mathsf{BG}$-0 noise with oracle complexity $O(\varepsilon^{-6})$. This rate holds both for standard smoothness and for $α$-symmetric generalized smoothness, showing that generalized smoothness is rate-neutral for normalized momentum in this setting. We then study a variance-reduced normalized STORM method. Under mean-square smoothness and sharp initialization, the method achieves the minimax optimal $O(\varepsilon^{-4})$ complexity, matching the lower bound. Under expected $α$-symmetric generalized smoothness, the STORM recursion couples gradient-dependent smoothness with distance-dependent noise, leading to complexity $O(\varepsilon^{-(4+α)})$ for $α\in(0,1)$ and $O(\varepsilon^{-5})$ for $α=1$. When the distance-growth parameter in the noise model vanishes, our guarantees recover the standard bounded-variance rates: $O(\varepsilon^{-4})$ for momentum, $O(\varepsilon^{-3})$ for variance reduction, and $O(\varepsilon^{-2})$ in the deterministic case. To our knowledge, these are the first convergence guarantees for normalized methods in non-convex stochastic optimization under $\mathsf{BG}$-0 noise without bounded domains, increasing batch sizes, or explicit anchoring, covering both standard and generalized smoothness regimes.

### [152] [From I/O to Code with Discovery Agent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15334)
*Yihong Dong,Jiaru Qian,Haoran Zhang,Peixu Wang,Binhua Li,Zhi Jin,Yongbin Li,Ge Li,Xiaokang Yang,Xue Jiang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DIO-Agent proposes an evolutionary search framework for IO2Code using LLMs as mutation operators guided by execution feedback. It incorporates the Transformation Priority Premise to favor simpler, evidence-consistent programs, improving efficiency and correctness. An IO2CodeBench is introduced for systematic evaluation, showing DIO-Agent outperforms existing methods across difficulty levels and LLMs.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The synthesis of programs from input-output examples (IO2Code) remains a challenging problem due to the vast, underspecified hypothesis space. Unlike NL2Code, which benefits from natural language-code alignment, IO2Code requires inferring underlying logic solely from behavior, making it fundamentally harder.

Method: DIO-Agent frames IO2Code as an evolutionary search over discrete program space. An LLM acts as a mutation operator, generating new candidate programs. Execution errors provide feedback to guide mutations. The Transformation Priority Premise is used as a prior to bias toward simpler constructs (e.g., constants before conditionals or loops), ensuring structural simplicity unless necessary.

Result: DIO-Agent consistently outperforms traditional program-by-example methods and state-of-the-art evolution-agent baselines across all difficulty levels in IO2CodeBench. It also surpasses test-time scaling strategies with the same sampling budget, demonstrating superior efficiency and effectiveness.

Conclusion: DIO-Agent provides a robust and principled approach to IO2Code by combining LLM-driven search with structured simplicity priors. The proposed benchmark enables systematic evaluation, paving the way for future advances in behavioral program synthesis.

Abstract: The automatic synthesis of a program from any form of specification is regarded as a holy grail of computer science. Fueled by LLMs, NL2Code has achieved tremendous success, yet the fundamentally more challenging task of synthesizing programs from input-output behavior, which we refer to as IO2Code, remains largely unsolved. Whereas NL2Code can exploit the semantic alignment between natural language and code acquired during pretraining, IO2Code requires recovering underlying principles from concrete computational behavior, navigating a vast and underspecified hypothesis space. To address this, we propose DIO-Agent, a discovery agent for IO2Code. Our method frames IO2Code as an evolutionary search over discrete program space, in which an LLM serves as the mutation operator and concrete error signals from execution guide each mutation. To prevent the search from wandering into structurally complex yet incorrect dead ends, we introduce the Transformation Priority Premise as a mutation prior that biases the LLM toward the simplest hypothesis consistent with current evidence, progressively escalating from constants to conditionals to iteration only when simpler constructs are insufficient. To facilitate systematic study, we further construct an IO2CodeBench spanning multiple difficulty levels. Extensive experiments show that DIO-Agent consistently outperforms both traditional program-by-example method and SOTA evolution-agent baselines across all difficulty levels and various LLMs, while substantially surpassing test-time scaling strategies with equivalent sampling budgets.

</details>


### [153] [Bounded-Rationality, Hedging, and Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15340)
*Pedro A. Ortega*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文将学习过程建模为有界理性决策问题，通过样本到输出的诱导信道分析学习者对训练数据的依赖程度与泛化能力之间的权衡。当响应律由f-散度正则化表示时，该框架在信息几何中生成下界交易曲线和上界证书曲线，其中KL散度对应香农互信息。通过观察对缩放损失和局部损失扰动的响应，可从黑箱行为中恢复出这种权衡关系。泛化被视作学习者响应律的可检验对冲性质，其有效性可通过恢复的对冲是否覆盖由特定训练样本引起的畸变来验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统泛化理论难以直接评估学习者对训练样本依赖性的实际影响，且缺乏可操作的验证机制。本文旨在建立一个可从黑箱行为中推断学习者泛化能力的理论框架，以提供可测试的泛化保证。

Method: 将学习过程视为有界理性决策问题，定义诱导信道作为基本对象；利用f-divergence正则化刻画响应律，构建基于信息几何的下界交易曲线与上界证书曲线；通过观测对缩放损失和局部扰动的响应，反推出学习者的对冲能力与畸变容忍度。

Result: 成功从黑箱行为中恢复出学习者的对冲能力与畸变容忍边界；提出了一种可检验的泛化测试方法：若恢复的对冲覆盖了样本引起的畸变，则认为该学习者具有良好的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 泛化不再是抽象的统计性质，而可转化为学习者自身响应律的可测试对冲属性。该框架为理解并验证机器学习模型的泛化能力提供了新视角与实用工具。

Abstract: A learner does not only fit data; it also determines how strongly the training sample may shape its output and how much distortion it can hedge. We study this relation as a bounded-rational decision problem whose primitive object is the induced channel from samples to outputs. The learner's response law determines which changes in this channel are cheap or costly, and therefore induces both a lower tradeoff curve between training loss and sample dependence and a matched upper certificate curve. When the response law is represented by an $f$-divergence regularizer, these curves live in the regularizer's native information geometry, with KL as the special case corresponding to Shannon mutual information. We show how the hedge and the two curves can be recovered from black-box behavior by observing responses to scaled losses and local loss perturbations. In learning, population loss is empirical loss plus the distortion induced by the particular training sample. The recovered hedge gives a practical certificate when it covers that distortion. Thus generalization is treated as a testable hedging property of the learner's own response law.

### [154] [LEAP: Trajectory-Level Evaluation of LLMs in Iterative Scientific Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15341)
*Marilyn Zhang,Tianfeng Chen,Fabián Barzuna,Ankita Rathod,Mark E. Whiting*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有迭代科学设计基准仅在固定时间点评估结果，忽略了学习轨迹，导致无法准确衡量学习效率。而学习效率直接影响成本和时间开销，因此需要更全面的评估方式。

Method: 提出LEAPBench框架，结合最佳当前结果的AUC轨迹指标、经典贝叶斯优化基线以及基于已发表文献的审计机制，对8个主流LLM进行系统评估，并探索轨迹度量作为强化学习奖励的有效性。

Result: 切换到轨迹评分后，53%的任务最佳模型决策发生变化；LLM未超越贝叶斯优化基线；领域无关提示在多数任务中表现更优；轨迹度量可有效提升离线强化学习性能，在14/21任务上实现改进。

Conclusion: 仅依赖最终结果的评估会误导对LLM学习效率的判断。轨迹评估能更真实反映模型进步过程，且其本身具备作为训练目标的潜力，有助于推动高效自主实验设计的发展。

Abstract: LLMs are increasingly deployed in autonomous laboratories, under the assumption that their domain priors and reasoning over iterative feedback let them converge on good designs in fewer iterations than feedback-only baselines. Current iterative scientific design benchmarks, however, score only outcome snapshots at fixed horizons. This leaves the learning trajectory unmeasured, even though the trajectory is what captures learning efficiency, where each iteration saved is a real saving in cost and time. Motivated by this, we examine three evaluation choices that change the conclusions one draws about LLM learning efficiency in iterative scientific design: what to measure, what baseline to compare against, and what to ground against. We introduce LEAPBench, Learning Efficiency in Adaptive Processes, a 55-task framework that pairs a best-so-far area under the curve (AUC) trajectory metric with a classical Bayesian-optimization reference and an audit grounded in published literature. Applied to eight contemporary LLMs, switching from final-outcome to trajectory scoring changes the best-model decision on 53% of tasks at matched horizons, and exposes efficiency gains overlooked by outcome-based scoring. LLMs do not outperform a classical Bayesian baseline. On 16 biology tasks where the oracle's reward signal is aligned with configurations from the published-best design, domain-aware prompting leads to LLM choices that match the published-best's approximately 10 percentage points less often than domain-agnostic prompting at iteration 30. The pattern is sharpest on 6 tasks where the literature-typical and published-best configurations diverge, and domain-agnostic prompting matches the published-best more often on all 6. The trajectory metric also doubles as a tractable training target. Offline reinforcement learning with the metric as a reward improves performance on 14 of 21 held-out tasks.

By learning a motif-aware graph space, CoMole transfers pretrained structural priors into controllable generation, where RL optimizes conditional reverse policies over chemically meaningful decisions. Abstract: Memory plays a central role in enabling large language models (LLMs) to operate over sequential tasks by accumulating and reusing experience over time. However, existing evaluations of LLM memory mostly rely on aggregate metrics such as final hold-out accuracy or cumulative online performance, which can obscure critical failure modes such as forgetting and negative transfer. In this paper, we introduce SeqMem-Eval, a diagnostic evaluation framework for sequentially evolving LLM memory. Drawing inspiration from continual learning, it targets a test-time setting in which memory is external, prompt-mediated, and updated without modifying model parameters. Rather than focusing only on final performance, SeqMem-Eval evaluates how memory states evolve, generalize, consolidate experience, and retain useful information during sequential inference. Specifically, it measures online utility, hold-out generalization, backward transfer, and forgetting, providing a finer-grained view of memory quality. Through extensive experiments across diverse tasks and memory methods, we show that higher final or cumulative accuracy does not necessarily imply better memory quality: many methods exhibit strong performance gains while suffering from substantial forgetting or negative transfer. Moreover, different memory designs exhibit distinct trade-offs between adaptability and stability that remain invisible under standard evaluation metrics.

### [157] [Unified High-Probability Analysis of Stochastic Variance-Reduced Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15388)
*Zhankun Luo,Antesh Upadhyay,M. Berk Sahin,Sang Bin Moon,Anuran Makur,Abolfazl Hashemi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一个统一的随机方差减少估计框架，基于包含记忆保留、重置概率和迭代移动修正项的递归结构。该框架可恢复多个经典估计器，启发新的二阶变体，并提供估计误差的偏差-方差分解。核心成果是使用新型无维度向量值Freedman不等式，建立适用于光滑赋范空间（包括欧氏与非欧氏情形）的统一高概率界，涵盖镜面下降在Banach空间中的分析。应用上，获得了无约束优化中镜面下降的高概率最优复杂度，对置信水平呈对数依赖；并首次得到带期望约束的随机优化的$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\varepsilon^{-3})$ oracle复杂度界，优于先前$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\varepsilon^{-4})$，首次引入方差减少估计于该场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法如动量、SPIDER、STORM、PAGE虽成功但分析依赖具体估计器且基于期望，缺乏对可靠性结构性权衡的揭示。亟需一种统一框架以理解不同估计器间的内在联系及性能边界。

Result: 建立了统一的高概率误差界，适用于多种优化设置；首次实现带期望约束的随机优化$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\varepsilon^{-3})$复杂度，显著优于原有$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\varepsilon^{-4})$；证明了镜面下降在高概率意义下的对数依赖复杂度。

Conclusion: 所提框架为随机方差减少估计提供了统一的理论视角，揭示了估计器设计中的关键结构权衡，推动了高概率复杂度分析的发展，尤其在非欧几何与约束优化中具有重要意义。

Abstract: Stochastic estimators are fundamental to large-scale optimization, where population quantities must be inferred from noisy oracle observations. Although influential methods such as momentum, SPIDER, STORM, and PAGE have been highly successful, their analyses are largely estimator-specific and expectation-based, obscuring the structural tradeoffs that determine reliability. In this paper, we develop a unified framework for stochastic variance-reduced estimation based on a recursion with three components: memory retention, reset probability, and a correction term for iterate movement. This framework recovers several classical estimators, motivates new second-order variants, and yields a bias-variance decomposition of estimation error. Our main result is a unified high-probability bound proved using a new dimension-free vector-valued Freedman inequality, valid for smooth normed spaces involving random sums of vector martingales. The result applies in both Euclidean and non-Euclidean settings, including the analysis of mirror-descent-based methods in Banach spaces. As applications, we obtain high-probability oracle complexities for unconstrained optimization with mirror descent, establishing the logarithmic dependence on the confidence level. We also derive the first $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\varepsilon^{-3})$ oracle-complexity bounds for stochastic optimization with expectation constraints, improving upon the existing $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\varepsilon^{-4})$ complexity by leveraging variance-reduced estimation for the first time in this setting.

### [158] [LPDS: Evaluating LLM Robustness Through Logic-Preserving Difficulty Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15393)
*Philipp Mondorf,Samuel J. Bell,Jesse Dodge,Dieuwke Hupkes*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为逻辑保持难度扩展（LPDS）的框架，用于系统性地识别在保持问题逻辑不变的前提下最可能导致大语言模型失败的变体。该框架量化问题变体的难度，并搜索允许的变体空间以发现最难的案例，从而更准确地评估模型的鲁棒性。实验表明，随着难度增加，模型性能下降，推理错误更加明显；与随机采样相比，LPDS能发现导致性能下降高达5倍的困难变体。此外，基于更难变体进行微调可带来更一致的鲁棒性提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型在面对逻辑相同但实体变化的问题时仍缺乏鲁棒性，而现有评估方法多依赖随机采样，无法有效识别最具挑战性的变体，容易高估模型性能。因此需要一种系统化的方法来发现并测试那些真正考验模型能力的变体。

Method: 提出逻辑保持难度扩展（LPDS）框架，通过量化问题变体的难度，并采用系统性搜索策略在允许的变体空间中寻找最大难度的样本，进而暴露模型弱点。同时结合微调实验验证不同难度训练数据对模型鲁棒性的提升效果。

Result: LPDS能够有效识别出导致模型性能显著下降的困难变体，其引发的性能下降幅度可达随机采样的5倍；在更难变体上进行微调后，模型表现出更强且更稳定的鲁棒性提升。

Conclusion: LPDS为评估和提升大语言模型在逻辑保持条件下的鲁棒性提供了一种高效、系统的方法，有助于推动模型向更可靠、更稳健的方向发展。

Abstract: As large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed to perform tasks with minimal human oversight, it is crucial that these models operate robustly. In particular, a model that can solve a given problem should not fail simply because certain entities$\unicode{x2013}$such as names, numbers, or other contextual details$\unicode{x2013}$have changed while the underlying problem logic remains the same. Prior work suggests that current LLMs still struggle with this form of robustness: they often succeed on some variations of a problem but fail on others. However, existing evaluations often lack a systematic way to identify which logic-preserving variations are most likely to induce failure. Instead, they typically test a random subset of allowable variations, which can overstate robustness. To address this gap, we introduce logic-preserving difficulty scaling (LPDS), a framework that (i) quantifies the difficulty of a problem variation and (ii) systematically searches the space of allowable variations to find those that maximize difficulty and expose failures. We show that as difficulty increases, performance declines and errors in the models' reasoning chains become more pronounced. We further demonstrate that LPDS efficiently finds difficult problem variations for a model, resulting in performance drops up to 5 times larger compared to random sampling. Finally, we show that fine-tuning on more difficult variations leads to more consistent robustness gains than training on easier ones.

</details>


### [159] [Representation Without Reward: A JEPA Audit for LLM Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15394)
*Biswa Sengupta*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究检验了在固定LoRA微调设置下，联合嵌入预测架构（JEPAs）在自然语言到正则表达式生成任务中的有效性。通过对比22种辅助目标，发现尽管某些方法在单细胞配对检验中表现出显著提升（如T3-Local在Δ=+2.53pp, p=0.003），但均未通过多重比较校正（Bonferroni或Holm-Bonferroni），表明结果不具统计稳健性。即使引入解码器可见的JEPA目标，虽首次获得正交交叉熵梯度余弦，但精确匹配仍被种子噪声掩盖。全量微调复现也得到类似零结果，说明隐藏状态几何与解码任务性能之间在该设定下耦合较弱。因此，研究提出应将大模型领域的JEPAs评估重新定义为‘耦合问题’，核心在于何种度量下有用隐藏结构可转化为解码器可见的任务信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究联合嵌入预测架构（JEPAs）在自回归语言模型微调中的有效性，特别是其是否能通过预测潜在表示来提升任务性能；重点考察隐藏状态几何与解码任务表现之间的耦合关系。

Method: 在固定Llama-3.2-1B-Instruct LoRA微调框架下，针对自然语言到正则表达式生成任务，系统测试22种训练时辅助目标，涵盖轨迹形状正则化、分布约束、预测器/目标不对称性、Fisher度量雅可比残差，以及新提出的解码器可见的JEPA目标。采用配对t检验和多重比较校正（Bonferroni/Holm-Bonferroni）评估效果，并进行全量微调复现以验证结果稳健性。

Result: 多个辅助目标在单变量检验中显示显著提升（如T3-Local），但均未通过多重比较校正；解码器可见的JEPA目标虽带来首个正交交叉熵梯度余弦，但精确匹配仍处于种子噪声水平；全量微调复现同样得到零结果，表明隐藏状态结构与解码任务性能之间在当前设定下耦合弱且不可靠。

Conclusion: 在当前实验设定下，隐藏状态表示与解码任务准确率之间存在弱耦合，提示应将大模型领域中JEPAs的评估重新定位为‘耦合问题’，即关注何种指标能有效将有用的隐藏几何转化为解码器可见的任务信号。

Abstract: Joint-embedding predictive architectures (JEPAs) propose that a model should learn more useful abstractions when trained to predict latent representations rather than observed outputs. For autoregressive language-model fine-tuning the principle entails a stricter requirement: the induced hidden-state geometry must reach the language-model head \emph{and} improve the decoded task metric. We test that requirement under a fixed Llama-3.2-1B-Instruct LoRA harness on natural-language-to-regex generation, comparing twenty-two training-time auxiliaries across trajectory-shape regularisation, distributional constraints, predictor/target asymmetry, Fisher-metric Jacobi residuals, and a decoder-visible JEPA objective constructed to lie in cross-entropy's positive cone. The empirical answer is a structured null: several auxiliaries clear single-cell paired $α= 0.10$ without correction (T3-Local at $Δ= +2.53$~pp, $p = 0.003$ being the strongest), but none survives Bonferroni or Holm--Bonferroni at the relevant family-wise threshold, even though many change curvature, anisotropy, variance, and gradient direction. Decoder-visible JEPA yields the first positive auxiliary--cross-entropy gradient cosine in the study, yet exact match remains inside seed noise; a full-fine-tuning replication of the same auxiliary at $n = 5$ seeds reproduces the null on both benchmarks (TURK: $Δ= +0.04$~pp, $p_{\text{paired}} = 0.96$; SYNTH: $Δ= +0.52$~pp, $p_{\text{paired}} = 0.28$), so the null is robust across LoRA and full fine-tuning for the decoder-visible construction. Hidden-state representation work and decoded-task accuracy are therefore weakly coupled in this regime; we accordingly reframe LLM-domain JEPA evaluation as a coupling problem, in which the operative question is under which metrics useful hidden geometry becomes decoder-visible task signal.

</details>


### [160] [Breakeven complexity: A new perspective on neural partial differential equation solvers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15399)
*Yijing Zhang,Nicholas Roberts,Tanya Marwah,Mikhail Khodak*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于断点复杂度的评估框架，用于更全面地衡量神经微分方程求解器在实际应用中的成本效益。该框架考虑了神经求解器训练和数据生成的前期开销，并与传统求解器在误差相当条件下的总成本进行比较，从而判断神经求解器何时变得经济高效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法仅关注精度，忽略了神经求解器在数据生成、训练和调优方面的高昂前期成本，以及传统求解器在低精度下仍可低成本运行的事实，因此需要一个能涵盖端到端成本的评估体系。

Method: 提出断点复杂度作为核心指标，结合尺度定律确定数据生成的训练预算，并通过平滑误差匹配策略适应不同场景，以实现公平对比。

Result: 在多个2D周期域上的PDE问题及多障碍物流场问题上测试表明，随着问题复杂度（如维度、雷诺数、模拟时长）增加，神经求解器相对于传统求解器的成本优势愈发明显。

Conclusion: 神经微分方程求解器在高成本、高复杂度任务中更具实用性，其性价比随问题难度提升而增强，断点复杂度是评估其真实价值的有效工具。

Abstract: Neural surrogate solvers of partial differential equations (PDEs) promise dramatic speedups over numerical methods, especially in scenarios requiring many solves. However, current accuracy-based evaluations do not fully consider two central issues: (1) neural solvers incur substantial up-front costs for data generation, training, and tuning; and (2) classical solvers can also generate low-fidelity solutions at a sufficiently low simulation cost. To explicitly account for these realities and fully incorporate end-to-end costs, we propose an evaluation framework centered on breakeven complexity, a metric that counts the forward solves before a learned solver is cost-effective relative to an error-equivalent traditional solver. To evaluate this measure, we apply scaling laws to determine how much training budget to allocate to data generation and discuss how to achieve smooth error-matching in diverse settings. We evaluate the breakeven complexity of multiple neural PDE solvers on three PDEs on 2D periodic domains from APEBench and a novel benchmark of flows past multiple obstacles generated by the GPU-native PyFR code. Among other findings, our results suggest that neural PDE solvers become more effective as problems get harder in terms of cost, dimension, rollout, physics regime (e.g. higher Reynolds number), etc.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有负载均衡方法多为启发式，基于噪声较大的小批量分配统计，相对于总体目标存在偏差，无法有效实现专家使用的平衡。

Method: 提出φ-平衡框架，通过最小化期望路由分布的严格凸、对称且可微的势能，结合凸对偶性和镜像下降，设计出高效的在线算法（EMA-based路由调整）。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models rely on balanced expert utilization to fully realize their scalability. However, existing load-balancing methods are largely heuristic and operate on noisy mini-batch assignment statistics, introducing bias relative to population-level objectives. We propose $φ$-balancing, a principled framework that directly targets population-level expert balance by minimizing a strictly convex, symmetric, and differentiable potential of the expected routing distribution. Using convex duality, we derive an equivalent min-max formulation and obtain a simple online algorithm via mirror descent, yielding an efficient EMA-based routing adjustment with negligible overhead. Across large-scale pretraining and downstream fine-tuning, $φ$-balancing consistently outperforms prior Switch-style and loss-free baselines, demonstrating more stable and effective expert utilization.

### [162] [Transformer Scalability Crisis: The First Comprehensive Empirical Analysis of Performance Walls in Modern Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15413)
*Mahdi Naser Moghadasi,Faezeh Ghaderi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文对118个不同架构的Transformer模型进行了大规模系统评估，揭示了其在可扩展性方面的根本性能瓶颈。研究发现，尽管88.1%的模型能处理512 token以内的序列，但在1024 token时成功率降至44.9%，2048 token时完全失败（0%）。压缩模型在参数效率上表现优异（649.2 tokens/sec/M），远超大型生成模型（12.5 tokens/sec/M）。结果表明，理论上的O(n²)注意力复杂度确实导致实际性能墙，挑战了现有缩放假设，并提出了新的基准测试方法，为生产部署提供关键参考。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对Transformer架构可扩展性的理解缺乏系统的实证分析，尤其在长序列处理方面存在明显性能瓶颈，亟需全面评估以揭示其真实限制。

Method: 采用系统化的基准测试方法，对118个Transformer模型在7种不同架构类别中进行跨序列长度（128至2048 token）的性能评估，分析加载时间、内存消耗与计算效率。

Result: 88.1%的模型可在512 token内正常运行，但该比例在1024 token时下降至44.9%，2048 token时为0%；压缩模型的参数效率显著优于大模型，验证了理论复杂度在实际中的影响。

Conclusion: Transformer模型存在明显的可扩展性瓶颈，其理论O(n²)注意力复杂度转化为实际部署中的硬性约束，必须重新审视现有缩放策略，并建立更科学的评估标准以指导实际应用。

Abstract: Despite the remarkable success of transformer architectures in natural language processing, their scalability limitations remain poorly understood through systematic empirical analysis. This paper presents the first comprehensive large-scale evaluation of 118 transformer models across seven distinct architectural categories, revealing fundamental performance walls that manifest as hard deployment constraints. Our systematic benchmarking methodology uncovers a critical scalability crisis: while 88.1% of models successfully process sequences up to 512 tokens, this drops dramatically to 44.9% at 1024 tokens, with complete failure (0%) at 2048 tokens. Through rigorous analysis of loading times, memory consumption, and computational efficiency across sequence lengths from 128 to 2048 tokens, we demonstrate that compressed models achieve superior parameter efficiency (649.2 tokens/sec/M parameters) compared to large generative models (12.5 tokens/sec/M). Our findings challenge prevailing scaling assumptions and provide the first quantitative evidence that the theoretical O(n2) attention complexity translates into measurable performance walls. This work establishes new benchmarking methodologies for transformer evaluation and provides critical insights for practical deployment decisions in production environments.

Abstract: Jung et al. (2025) introduce a hypothesis testing framework for guaranteeing agreement between large language models (LLMs) and human judgments, relying on the assumption that the model's estimated confidence is monotonic with respect to human-disagreement risk. In practice, however, this assumption may be violated, and the generalization behavior of the confidence estimator is not explicitly analyzed. We mitigate these issues by learning a dedicated confidence estimator instead of relying on heuristic confidence signals. Our approach leverages simulated annotator diversity and a margin-based ranking formulation to explicitly model how confidently an LLM distinguishes between human-agreement and human-disagreement cases. We further derive generalization guarantees for this estimator, revealing a margin-dependent trade-off that informs the design of an adaptive estimator training procedure. ### [164] [Lagrangian Flow Matching: A Least-Action Framework for Principled Path Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15419)
*Shukai Du,Junzhe Zhang,Yiming Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于物理的流匹配框架——拉格朗日流匹配，通过最小化一般拉格朗日量的作用量来确定概率路径和速度场，克服了传统方法仅依赖直线路径的局限性。该方法在保持与最优传输等价的基础上，引入更丰富的动态行为，支持新路径设计，并在实验中展现出与现有模型相当甚至更优的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有流匹配方法使用的概率路径（如直线或最优传输路径）仅覆盖有限的动态类型，其背后对应经典力学中最简单的自由粒子运动。为拓展可建模的动力学范围，需引入更一般的物理原理指导路径设计。

Method: 基于最小作用量原理，构建以一般拉格朗日量为基础的动态优化问题，结合连续性方程与边界条件求解概率路径与速度场；进一步证明其等价于静态最优传输问题，从而导出无需模拟的训练目标。

Result: 所提方法能生成多样化的概率路径，涵盖最优传输（动能项）与三角方差保持扩散路径（谐振子项）等特例；数值实验表明新路径显著改变学习到的动力学，且性能不逊于现有条件流匹配模型。

Conclusion: 拉格朗日流匹配提供了一个统一、可扩展的框架，将物理规律融入生成建模中，使流匹配从几何构造迈向动力学建模，为复杂数据分布的学习提供了新的可能性。

Abstract: Flow matching trains a neural velocity field by regression against a target velocity associated with a prescribed probability path connecting a simple initial distribution to the data distribution. A central design choice is the path itself. Existing constructions, including rectified and optimal-transport-based paths, transport samples along straight lines between coupled endpoints and thus cover only a narrow class of dynamics. We observe that this corresponds to the simplest case of the least-action principle in classical mechanics, in which the kinetic Lagrangian yields free-particle straight-line trajectories. Building on this observation, we propose Lagrangian flow matching, a physics-based framework in which the probability path and velocity field are determined by minimizing the action of a general Lagrangian subject to the continuity equation and the prescribed endpoints. We show that this dynamic problem admits an equivalent static optimal transport (OT) formulation, yielding a family of simulation-free training objectives that recover OT-based flow matching as the kinetic special case and the trigonometric variance-preserving diffusion path as the harmonic-oscillator case. More general Lagrangians give rise to new probability paths and velocity fields, and numerical experiments show that they induce meaningful changes in the learned dynamics while remaining competitive with existing conditional flow matching models.

Abstract: Electroencephalograph (EEG) timeseries signals are characterized by significant noise and coarse spatial resolution, which complicates the classification of neurodegenerative diseases. Even SOTA deep learning architectures struggle to distinguish between healthy controls and diseased subjects, or between different disease types, due to high intergroup similarity. In this paper, we show that a spectrally selective approach to feature construction enhances class separability. By isolating signal strengths within the primary brainwave bands, we transform high dimensional raw data into high value spectral features. Our results demonstrate that a) features derived from frequency and time frequency domain allow traditional machine learning models to match or exceed the performance of SOTA deep learning models, b) Attention mechanism is unable to distill the stable feature signatures that characterize healthy neural activity in both resting and task EEGs, and c) the limitations of attention based models in finding relevant spectral features appear to be fundamental in that providing frequency selective time domain input do not appreciably improve their performance. ### [166] [Layer-wise Derivative Controlled Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15463)
*Rowan Martnishn,Sean Anderson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ChainzRule (CR) is a novel neural architecture that balances accuracy, hardware efficiency, and functional stability by replacing piecewise-linear activations with a Polynomial Engine guided by Differential Regularization (DREG). DREG targets intermediate derivatives to suppress sensitivity without sacrificing representational power. CR achieves superior performance with 15.5x fewer parameters, reduces gradient volatility by 23.1% on MNIST, and attains 70.17% accuracy on Yelp ordinal regression, proving that stability and high performance can coexist.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing machine learning models face conflicting demands: high accuracy, hardware efficiency, and functional stability. Traditional architectures often sacrifice stability for performance, leading to unpredictable outputs under small input changes—especially problematic in sensitive real-world applications.

Method: ChainzRule replaces standard activations with a Polynomial Engine and applies Differential Regularization (DREG), which acts as targeted regularization on intermediate derivatives rather than imposing global Lipschitz constraints. This preserves model expressiveness while suppressing extreme sensitivity.

Result: In benchmark tests, ChainzRule outperformed standard models with 15.5x fewer parameters. On MNIST, it reduced peak gradient volatility by 23.1%. On Yelp Full ordinal regression, it achieved 70.17% accuracy under explicit DREG regularization, demonstrating compatibility with real-world tasks.

Conclusion: By embedding derivative awareness into the architecture via DREG, ChainzRule proves that functional stability and high accuracy are not mutually exclusive, offering a new paradigm for robust, efficient, and reliable neural network design.

Abstract: As machine learning models grow in complexity, they increasingly struggle with three conflicting demands: the need for high accuracy, the requirement for hardware efficiency, and the necessity of functional stability. Traditional architectures often achieve performance at the expense of spiky or unpredictable behavior, where small changes in input lead to massive swings in output -- a critical flaw for real-world deployment in sensitive environments. This paper introduces ChainzRule (CR), a novel neural architecture designed to harmonize these competing goals. ChainzRule replaces standard piecewise-linear activations with a Polynomial Engine governed by Differential Regularization (DREG). Unlike traditional methods that impose global, coarse-grained constraints on a model's Lipschitz constant, DREG acts as a targeted regularization on intermediate derivatives. This approach suppresses extreme sensitivity without attenuating the representational power inherent in the Polynomial Engine. In head-to-head "Fair Fight" benchmarks, ChainzRule outperformed standard models while using 15.5x fewer parameters. On the MNIST dataset, it reduced peak gradient volatility by an average of 23.1%, ensuring a smoother and more predictable manifold. On Yelp Full ordinal regression under explicit DREG regularization, ChainzRule achieves 70.17% accuracy, validating that derivative-aware regularization is compatible with competitive performance on realistic tasks. By embedding gradient awareness into the architecture via DREG, ChainzRule demonstrates that stability and accuracy need not be competing objectives.

### [167] [GRLO: Towards Generalizable Reinforcement Learning in Open-Ended Environments from Zero](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15464)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于验证器的强化学习（RLVR）虽在特定任务上表现优异，但需大量GPU算力，限制了广泛应用。本文旨在探索少量人类反馈训练的RLHF是否能通过隐式迁移，有效提升模型在数学推理与代码生成等任务上的表现，从而降低训练成本并增强泛化能力。

Method: 采用小规模人类反馈数据在开放环境进行强化学习（RLHF）训练，学习对话能力；随后评估该能力是否可隐式迁移到数学推理、代码生成等下游任务，形成一种高效且具备广泛适应性的后训练范式——GRLO。

Result: 在Qwen3-4B-Base模型上，GRLO仅用5000个提示和22.7 GPU小时，使多领域平均性能从24.1提升至63.1，相比强基线节省46倍数据与68倍算力；模型性能甚至接近官方发布的大规模后训练模型。后续加入域内RLVR仅在困难竞赛类数学题上带来局部提升。

Conclusion: GRLO提供了一种简单高效的后训练策略，利用小规模人类反馈训练获得的对话能力可有效隐式迁移至复杂推理任务，显著降低计算成本，具有广阔的应用前景。

Abstract: Post-training has become a crucial step for unlocking the capabilities of large language models, with reinforcement learning (RL) emerging as a critical paradigm. Recent RL-based post-training has increasingly split into two paradigms: reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF), which optimizes models using human preference signals in target domains, and reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR), which operates in verifier-backed environments. The latter has dominated recent reasoning-oriented post-training because it delivers stronger gains and higher efficiency on domain-specific tasks (e.g., reasoning). However, although in-domain RL training achieves promising performance, it still requires a substantial amount of GPU compute, which remains a major barrier to broad adoption. In this work, we study the generalization ability of RLHF learned from scratch from a small set of interactions in open-ended environments, and investigate whether the conversational abilities it explicitly acquires can implicitly transfer to downstream tasks such as mathematical reasoning and code generation, namely GRLO. Specifically, on Qwen3-4B-Base backbone, GRLO improves the average performance across all domains from 24.1 to 63.1 with only 5K prompts and 22.7 GPU hours, requiring about $46\times$ less data and $68\times$ less compute than a strong in-domain RLVR baseline. The resulting model is even competitive with Qwen's released post-trained models which required a much larger training cost. Notably, a subsequent in-domain RLVR stage brings only selective gains, mainly on harder competition-math benchmarks. We hope GRLO offers a simple and efficient recipe for building broadly capable post-trained models. Our code and data will be available at: \href{https://github.com/SJY8460/GRLO}{https://github.com/SJY8460/GRLO}.

*Yunfei Luo,Xi Chen,Yuliang Chen,Lanshuang Zhang,Md Mofijul Islam,Siwei Zhao,Peter Kotanko,Subhasis Dasgupta,Andrew Campbell,Rakesh Malhotra,Tauhidur Rahman*

Method: NormWear-2 将多变量生理信号与临床干预变量编码至共享隐空间，建模其作为动力系统联合演化；结合预训练先验知识（直觉）与即时非参数隐状态转移适应（洞察），实现跨时间尺度的一致性预测；预训练阶段引入混沌理论优化动态模式多样性以增强表示鲁棒性。

Result: NormWear-2 在多个真实世界生理数据集上表现优异，涵盖不同时间分辨率和干预模式，涉及健身规划、透析、糖尿病管理、手术监测等场景；在时间、频率和隐空间三个维度均达到最佳预测性能，显著超越当前最先进的时序基础模型，且保持良好的下游表示质量。

Abstract: Physiological time series signals reflect complex, multi-scale dynamical processes of the human body. Existing modeling studies focus on static tasks such as classification, event forecasting, or short-horizon next step prediction, while long-horizon signal-level forecasting and predictive nature of physiological signals remain underexplored. We introduce NormWear-2, a world model that encodes both multivariate physiological signals and clinical intervention variables into a shared latent space and models their joint temporal evolution as a dynamical system. Our approach combines inference from prior pre-trained knowledge (intuition) with instant non-parametric latent state transition adaptation (insight), enabling coherent forecasting across multiple temporal scales, conditioned on heterogeneous clinical interventions. During the pretraining phase, we find that chaos-theoretic balancing of dynamical regime diversity yields more robust representations, with a smaller balanced corpus outperforming one twice its size and capturing bifurcation regimes. We evaluate the world model performance across diverse real-world physiological datasets spanning heterogeneous temporal resolutions and intervention regimes, covering daily life, point-of-care, and clinical settings, including fitness planning, hemodialysis, diabetes management, and surgical monitoring. These evaluation datasets comprise records from 8,026 subjects, spanning study durations from 3.2 hours for high-resolution signal data to 2.3 years for longitudinal clinical biomarker tracking. NormWear-2 achieves the best overall forecasting performance across time, frequency, and latent representation domains, with significant improvements over state-of-the-art time series foundation models, while maintaining competitive downstream representation quality, providing a step toward general-purpose world models for physiological signals.

Current solution approaches require ML systems to implement protocols to mitigate their biases. However, ML system owners usually do not have any incentive to implement these protocols and often argue that it limits their freedom of expression or business. We believe that a successful solution to this problem must recognize the conflict of interest between the ML systems and their users, and use this information to protect users against information that adversely influences their decisions while allowing users to safely benefit from these systems. To this end, we propose a game-theoretic framework that models the interaction between ML systems and users with conflicts of interest. We present scalable algorithms with theoretical guarantees that maximize the amount of desired information and actions and minimize the amount of biased and manipulative actions in interaction with ML systems.

### [171] [parallelcbf: A composable safety-filter and auditability framework for tensor-parallel reinforcement learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15509)
*Yijun Lu,Zilei Yang,Yuyin Ma*
